       <script>
        $(".ls-slide a").click(function(){
    var lsindex = $(this).closest(".ls-slide").index(".ls-slide");
    var lspos = lsindex+1;
    var lsOrd;
    switch (lspos) {
      case 1:
        lsOrd = "primo";
        break;
      case 2:
        lsOrd = "secondo";
        break;
      case 3:
        lsOrd = "terzo";
        break;
      case 4:
        lsOrd = "quarto";
        break;
      case 5:
        lsOrd = "quinto";
        break;
      case 6:
        lsOrd = "sesto";
        break;
    }
    ga('send', 'event', 'slider banner', 'click', lsOrd);
    //alert("clicked banner: " + lsOrd);
  });
       </script>

         $(document).ready(function(){
    $(".whychoose .col-xs-12").hover(
      function() {
        $(this).find('.imghover').stop().animate({"opacity": "0"}, "fast");

        <script type="text/javascript">
         $(document).ready(function(){
    var widthslide = 370;  
    var marginslide = 30;
    var slidesmax = 3;
    var widthwrap = $(".homepage > .container").width();
    var view = "LG";
    var Nview = "";
    //console.log (widthwrap);
    if (widthwrap <= 940 && widthwrap >= 721) {
      widthslide = 293;  
      slidesmax = 3;
      view = "MD";
    };
    if (widthwrap <= 720 && widthwrap >= 481) {
      widthslide = 345;
      slidesmax = 2;
      view = "SM";
    };
    //$(".bxsliderprodotti li").css('width', widthslide + 'px');
    if (widthwrap < 480) {
      widthslide = 0;
      marginslide = 15;
      slidesmax = 1;
      view = "XS";
    };
    var slideprodotti = $('.bxslider').bxSlider({
      autoStart: true,
      pause: 8000,
      pager: false,
      minSlides: 1,
      maxSlides: slidesmax,
      moveSlides: 1,
      slideWidth: widthslide,
      slideMargin: marginslide,
      onSliderLoad: function(){ $(".whychoose").css("visibility","visible"); }
    });
    $(window).resize(function() {
      var Rwidthwrap = $(window).width();
      // la width pare leggere anche 17px della scrollbar
      if (Rwidthwrap > 1182) {
        widthslide = 370; 
        marginslide = 30;
        slidesmax = 3;
        Nview = "LG";
      };
      if (Rwidthwrap <= 1182 && Rwidthwrap > 974) {
        widthslide = 293; 
        marginslide = 30;
        slidesmax = 3;
        Nview = "MD";
      };
      if (Rwidthwrap <= 974 && Rwidthwrap > 463) {
        widthslide = 345;
        marginslide = 30;
        slidesmax = 2;
        Nview = "SM";
      };
      if (Rwidthwrap <= 463) {
        widthslide = 0;
        marginslide = 15;
        slidesmax = 1;
        Nview = "XS";
      };
      //console.log ("v" + view);
      //console.log ("N" + Nview);
      if (Nview != "" && Nview != view ) {
        view = Nview;
        slideprodotti.reloadSlider({
          autoStart: true,
          pause: 8000,
          pager: false,
          minSlides: 1,
          maxSlides: slidesmax,
          moveSlides: 1,
          slideWidth: widthslide,
          slideMargin: marginslide
        });
      };
    });
  });
        </script>

     ibody.css({ 'width' : '100%' });
     //ibody.width( $(this).width() + 20 ); //remove scrollbar by adding width
     $('.tweetnews').css({ 'height' : '100px'});
  } //endif
})
});



  function hideTwitterBoxElements() {
    setTimeout( function() {
      if ( $('[id*=twitter-widget-0]').length ) {
        $('[id*=twitter-widget-0]').each( function(){
         
     var ibody = $(this).contents().find( 'body' );
          if ( ibody.find('li.timeline-TweetList-tweet' ).length ) {	 
            ibody.find('li.timeline-TweetList-tweet:first').show();
            $('[id*=TwitterBlock]').css({ 'visibility' : 'visible' });
            $('[class*=tweetnews]').height('100px');
          }
          else {
            $(this).hide();
          }
        });
      }
      hideTwitterAttempts++;
      if ( hideTwitterAttempts < 3 ) {
        hideTwitterBoxElements();
      }
    }, 2000);
  }
  
  $(document).ready(function() {
    hideTwitterBoxElements();
    setInterval( function() {
      var ibody = $('#twitter-widget-0').contents().find('body');
      ibody.find('li.timeline-TweetList-tweet:first').fadeOut().appendTo(ibody.find('ol.timeline-TweetList'));
      ibody.find('li.timeline-TweetList-tweet:first').fadeIn(); 
    }, 5000); 
  });
//]]>
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>

   <script language="javascript">
    //<!-- Auto Open -->
setTimeout(function () {
  if (document.cookie.replace(/(?:(?:^|.*;\s*)OpenChatControl\s*\=\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$/, "$1") !== "true") {
	var $verty = $(".chatslider");
	$verty.delay(10000).animate({
	  bottom: parseInt($verty.css('bottom'), 10) == 174 ?
	  $verty.outerHeight() :
	  174
	}, 1000);
	$(".chatslider-tab-up").hide(5);
	$(".chatslider-tab-down").hide(5).delay(12000).fadeIn(5);
	document.cookie = "OpenChatControl=true;";
  }
});
//<!-- Display Block -->
$(".chatslider").css('display', 'block');
//<!-- Open and Closed function -->
$(".chatslider-tab-up").click(function () {
  var $verty = $(".chatslider");
  $verty.animate({
	bottom: parseInt($verty.css('bottom'), 10) == 174 ?
	$verty.outerHeight() :
	174
  });
  $(".chatslider-tab-up").hide();
  $(".chatslider-tab-down").show();
});
$(".chatslider-tab-down").click(function () {
  var $verty = $(".chatslider");
  $verty.animate({
	bottom: parseInt($verty.css('top'), 10) == 174 ?
	-$verty.outerHeight() :
	0
  });
  $(".chatslider-tab-down").hide();
  $(".chatslider-tab-up").show();
});
//<!-- Open Live Chat PopUp Window -->
var chat= function (selector) {
  if (typeof chat.w == 'undefined') {
	chat.w = {};
  }
  $(selector).click(function (e) {
	e.preventDefault();
	if (typeof $(this).attr("target") == 'undefined' || $(this).attr("target").toLowerCase() != "_blank") {
	  $(this).attr("target", "_blank");
	}            
	var bc = $("body").attr("class"), rel = $(this).attr("rel");
	(bc != "undefined" && bc != "") ? wn = bc.replace(new RegExp(" ", 'g'), "").toLowerCase() + rel : wn = rel;
	var wh = $(this).attr("href"), w = 560, h = 600;                    
	if (typeof chat.w[wn] == 'undefined' || chat.w[wn].closed) {
	  var p = 'toolbar=0,scrollbars=1,location=0,statusbar=0,menubar=0,resizable=1,width='+w+',height='+h;
	  chat.w[wn] = window.open(wh, wn, p);
	  chat.w[wn].moveTo(250, 250);
	  chat.w[wn].resizeTo(w, h);
	} else {
	  chat.w[wn].focus();
	}
	return false;
  });
}
chat("a[rel='livechat nofollow']");
   </script>

   <!-- Begin Top Links functions -->
   <script type="text/javascript">
    /* Top Links functions */
    
    /* close each panel */
    function closeTopPanels() {
      $('.top-toggle-bar').each(function(i, obj) { 
        if ($(this).css('display') == 'block') {
          $(this).slideToggle();
          var btn = '#' + $(this).attr('id').replace('-bar', '-toggle');
          $(btn).removeClass('active');
        }
      });
    }
    
    /* open Services menu -> hide hamburger */
    $('#btn-xs-mainnav').click(function () {
      closeTopPanels();
      if($('#xs-top-toggle').hasClass('in')) {
        $('#xs-top-toggle').collapse('hide'); 
        $('#btn-xs-toggle').addClass('collapsed');
      }
    });
    
    /* open Hamburger menu -> hide Services */
    $('#btn-xs-toggle').click(function () {
      closeTopPanels();
      if($('#main-menu').hasClass('in')) {
        $('#main-menu').collapse('hide'); 
        $('#btn-xs-mainnav').addClass('collapsed');
      }
    });
    
    /* slide XS */
    function slideTopPanel(button) {
      button = '#' + button;
      var panel = $(button).attr('href');
      
      $('.top-toggle-bar').each(function(i, obj) { // toggle panel except current
        if ($(this).css('display')== 'block' && $(this).attr('id') != panel.substring(1)) {
          $(this).slideToggle();
          var btn = '#' + $(this).attr('id').replace('-bar', '-toggle');
          $(btn).removeClass('active');
        }
      });
      $(button).toggleClass('active');   
      $(panel).delay(500).slideToggle();
    }
    
    /* slide XXS */
    function slideTopPanelXxs(button) {
      button = '#' + button;
      var panel = $(button).attr('href');
      $(button).toggleClass('active');     
      $(panel).animate({width: 'toggle'});
    }
    
    /* close XXS panel*/
    $('.close-panel-xxs').click(function () {
      var btn = $(this).parent().attr('id').replace('-bar', '-toggle');
      slideTopPanelXxs(btn);
    });
    
    /* open XS or XXS panel */
    $('.btn-toggle').click(function () {
      if($('body').hasClass('viewport-xxs')){
        slideTopPanelXxs($(this).attr('id'));
      }
      else {
        slideTopPanel($(this).attr('id'));
      }
      
    });
   </script>
   <!-- End Top Links functions -->
